üõè „ÄêÔ∏èBeijing Jinyu Badaling Crowne Plaza Hotel Check-in Guide„Äë

üìå Hotel Overview

‚ù∂. Comprehensive evaluation: The hotel is tailor-made for the Winter Olympics. Two years ago, it was praised by the Winter Olympics media reporters. Today, this good reputation is still spreading. IHG's rapid development in China has left all competitors far behind. On the 18th of this month, Nanjing Jiangbei Wanhuicheng Holiday Inn Express was grandly reopened! Even if we go back to the "Crowne Plaza" brand, the layout in Greater China has reached as many as 123. Obviously, the new hotels that have sprung up like mushrooms after the rain will take Badaling CP as a template and example. The points they need to learn include: accurate positioning, standardized management, complete supporting facilities, and dedicated employees.

üè® About the guest room In Room

‚ù∂. Guest room layout: The richness of welcome fruits exceeds that of most InterContinental hotels in Beijing (we have checked in at all 31 InterContinental hotels in Beijing, so we have a say); the unique welcome desserts are combined with local architectural features, which is a clever idea worth appreciating. This is our fifth stay at Badaling CP. We have previously experienced the 80-square-meter luxury suite and the parent-child suite. This time we experienced the 120-square-meter executive suite. The bar, dining table, washbasin, double bathroom, air purifier, humidifier, etc. are all particularly suitable for large families. As a state-owned enterprise directly managed by the Beijing State-owned Assets Supervision and Administration Commission, the famous Jinyu itself started with its main business of building materials. Therefore, the hardware construction quality of Badaling CP is outstanding, and even if you nitpick, you can't find any faults.

‚òïÔ∏è Dining

‚ù∂. Gourmet glimpse: The Chinese restaurants of InterContinental Hotel, the larger one is called Caifenglou, and the more refined one is called Caifeng Restaurant. In any case, the products have never disappointed: the authentic Yunnan cuisine of Kunming Huayi, the plus version of stinky mandarin fish of Huailai CP, the flavorful and dense pressed pot abalone potato chicken of Badaling Crowne Plaza... all left a deep and beautiful impression on people's taste buds and body and mind. Especially Manager Shang of Badaling CP Caifeng Restaurant, he took good care of my son. This is the dream of a home away from home. I have to give him a thumbs up. The full-time restaurant supervisors Jason, Manager Duan, Lily, Yucia, Mike, etc., without exception, have all been diligent, natural, and thoughtful (for example, they close quickly, serve with a smile from the heart, and knowing that I love scallion pancakes, they specially bring it to me...). I have stayed in all 6 Crowne Plaza hotels in Beijing, and this is the first time I have seen such an excellent Western food team. The last one that made us feel amazed was the Hyatt Regency Wangjing. In horizontal comparison, the friendly staff of Badaling CP are no less than any other hotel - it is impossible to be unhappy in such a hotel. The restaurant has a diamond member area. An ice bucket is thoughtfully prepared next to the freshly ground coffee machine for breakfast. The coffee beans are "Milan Gold Medal" with a good and mellow taste; the volcanic stone grilled sausages are solid. Like Crowne Plaza Yiwu and Xining Hot Spring Holiday, the "happy hour" of administrative trea**ent will be upgraded to a buffet for free, which is very cost-effective. Buffets are often themed. Not long ago, there was barbecue, and recently it was Southeast Asian style. In short, even long-term guests will not feel bored. As an international hotel group with a strong sense of social responsibility, the love of InterContinental hotels is diffused in every corner you can perceive. For example, among the restaurant staff, this Crowne Plaza has made an exception to recruit some smart and job-seeking deaf-mute people ("Ele.me" is also doing similar good deeds). The small details here can feel the warmth of the entire team. I am still moved when I think about it.

üèä Hardware Facilities

‚ù∂. Hotel environment: The executive lounge has been changed to a children's activity center, and the presidential suite has been changed to a baby care center. The relevant children's activities are extremely rich. There will be exhibition boards in the lobby to make relevant clear instructions-it is not Club Med, but better than Club Med. Here, parents can rest assured and leave the responsibility of walking the baby to the hotel. The lobby does not adopt a large and magnificent style, but instead caters to the natural leisure style of the bamboo forest, which is particularly suitable for the scene and is also particularly suitable for punching in. The lobby bar afternoon tea has a wide variety of dishes, and the desserts are of high quality. The steps of the lobby bar will be transformed into a stage and stands at night, and there are often performances (such as shadow puppetry, etc.), which are deeply loved by children. The greening of the park has reached perfection. Although there are complete fitness facilities on the second floor, I still recommend that everyone take a walk or morning exercise in the park. The towering mountains and the surging Guihe River are accompanied by nature, which is very enjoyable.

üåü Unforgettable Moments
1. Outstanding performance and awards of star employees (whether the service is strong): From top to bottom, whether it is middle and senior management or grassroots employees, they can all call my name. Obviously, they have undergone rigorous training. Our private butler Melody (Manager Han) arranged everything in detail, from the preparation of children's bathroom supplies to the upgrade of the room, etc. With such a caring person, I feel that the hotel is like my own home, comfortable, refreshing, and full of sunshine. No matter how many unsatisfactory things you have in life, you can easily solve them at Badaling CP, because there is a group of benchmark employees who are like Melody and serve with the most sincere attitude.

üìç Brief summary Conclusion

1. Wonderful moments of the journey: Yanqing is one of the venues for the Winter Olympics, and there are many ski resorts around. As the official reception hotel for the Olympics, the hotel will also hold various ice and snow activities in winter, such as turning the small garden into a snow ring field; in summer, it is about 5 degrees lower than the city, which is especially suitable for summer vacation. The "Summer Capital" is indeed worthy of its reputation. The hotel's outdoor entertainment projects include: karts, super slides, basketball, cruise ships, swings, trampolines, etc.; indoor entertainment projects include: hot springs, swimming pools, Bada Amusement Park, electronic amusement halls, children's playgrounds, table tennis, table football, billiards, etc. In the off-season, the hotel will gather the guest rooms on the 7th floor, and when it is full, the 6th floor will be opened, and so on. This is environmentally friendly and easy to manage (in addition to the good view, important facilities are all on the top floor, such as the 240-square-meter presidential suite and the executive lounge, etc.); in the peak season, it is difficult to find a room, and you need to book in advance. There are many attractions and shopping places around the hotel. It takes 5 minutes to drive to Wanda, 15 minutes to Longqing Gorge (there is a Sinopec gas station on the way), and half an hour to Badaling.

msg:After the epidemic, I have been looking for good parent-child hotels in Beijing and its surrounding areas, but there are very few suitable ones. After discovering Crowne Plaza Hebei Zunhua on May 1st and actually checking in and having an extraordinary experience, this week I discovered another treasure under the brand, Crowne Plaza Beijing Jinyu Badaling. I can't wait to book the experience. The comments are as follows:

The location, the hotel is backed by Badaling, adjacent to the Guishui River, and enjoys the natural beauty of "the city is in the garden, the city and the scenery blend together". There are children's paradise, children's trains and karts (all need to be paid separately), so that guests can enjoy the healing and parent-child friendly experience without going out of the park. If you come by car, you can reach the Beijing-Tibet Expressway and the Jingli Expressway, which is very convenient. Due to the World Horticultural Exhibition and the Winter Olympics, the surrounding roads are very well repaired!

For sightseeing, there are many famous scenic spots around, including Badaling Great Wall, Longqingxia Scenic Area, Wild Duck Lake National Wetland Park, Shiyuan Park, etc., all within half an hour's drive.

For dining, the hotel is within walking distance to Wanda Plaza and Wal-Mart shopping district (20-25 minutes), which is convenient for dining and shopping. There are 3-4 Chinese and Western restaurants in the hotel, with authentic taste and high cost performance.

Facilities fully reflect the resort-style design concept and the standardized temperament of Crowne Plaza International five-star hotel. 7 storeys high, low density, simple and elegant overall, integrated with the surrounding harmonious natural environment, the lobby is modern and modern style, beautifully decorated, the layout of the room is reasonable (big bed and sofa bed), comfortable bedding, comfortable living .

Children's activities are detailed and rich in content. There are different activities every day. On weekends, we participated in facial portraits, card issuance, mortise and tenon joints, lottery draws, fluid bears, outdoor production, and kite flying. We really enjoyed it and were overwhelmed.

Service, this is the most worth mentioning. Every service staff in the store is lovely and courteous, especially Xiao Ai at the front desk, who provided us with meticulous and considerate services. Before the trip, he gave me a detailed introduction to the hotel situation, children's activity time and various precautions. After check-in, he asked me many times about the check-in experience to find out if there were any problems that needed help and solutions. It fully embodies the customer-oriented service concept and the brand soft power of Crowne Plaza. The whole family is deeply impressed and very moved...

This must be a place that you should come to. I still want to come here after leaving. I will definitely come again in the future. I recommend everyone to come to a family-friendly resort hotel! ! !

Transportation: It takes one and a half to two hours on the road, which is really far. It is very interesting to pass through the Changcheng District in the middle. There is Wanda around the hotel. It is a 15-minute walk and it is convenient to eat.
Environment: The room is very spacious and very new. The hot spring is similar to a private soup. It is a small room and a small room. Because it is newly opened, it is very clean. , The steaming area and the swimming area are very few and clean. The children's water park is suitable for small babies. If the children are small, it is recommended to go directly to the water park in the hot spring. The water in the swimming area is cooler.
Hygiene: Both the room and the hot spring swimming are very clean. Bulgari bathing is used in the hot spring area. There is a sufficient supply of mineral water bath towels, which can be replaced at any time. This is really very good.
Service: The staff are enthusiastic. The staff who encounter the elevator will interact with the children to say hello and introduce the facilities. The staff in each area will also take the initiative to solve the problem.
Disadvantages: There are few varieties of breakfast, basically all parent-child activities are charged separately, unless you buy a package
As a parent-child hotel, it is still very good and worth a visit

swimming pool:
